HRC Dark Reference

This one SBC superdark is used for all SBC data. See the reference file delivery logsheet for more information. This file can be downloaded directly from the jref directory.

To retrieve a file from the archive, click in the file name. For details on how to correctly set up the Archive retrieval options for reference files, check our Help page.

To receive e-mail notifications of deliveries of new reference files, you can subscribe to instrument specific mailing lists. More.

See the reference file delivery logsheet for more information. These files can also be downloaded directly from the jref directory. If you choose to access the files via this ftp server, keep in mind that there is a known bug in trying to access files via ftp server using Safari. The recommended browser is Firefox.
